﻿using System;

namespace Logic.Events
{
	// Token: 0x0200005E RID: 94
	public class EventWrapper<T> : IDisposable
	{
		// Token: 0x1700004C RID: 76
		// (get) Token: 0x060002F5 RID: 757 RVA: 0x00012BAB File Offset: 0x00010DAB
		// (set) Token: 0x060002F6 RID: 758 RVA: 0x00012BB3 File Offset: 0x00010DB3
		public T value
		{
			get
			{
				return this._value;
			}
			set
			{
				this._value = value;
				if (this._value == null)
				{
					this._value = this._default;
				}
			}
		}

		// Token: 0x060002F7 RID: 759 RVA: 0x00012BD5 File Offset: 0x00010DD5
		public EventWrapper(T defaultValue)
		{
			this._default = defaultValue;
			this._value = this._default;
		}

		// Token: 0x060002F8 RID: 760 RVA: 0x00012BF0 File Offset: 0x00010DF0
		public void Dispose()
		{
			this._default = default(T);
			this._value = default(T);
		}

		// Token: 0x0400054D RID: 1357
		private T _default;

		// Token: 0x0400054E RID: 1358
		private T _value;
	}
}

		// Token: 0x0600075F RID: 1887 RVA: 0x0001C5CC File Offset: 0x0001A7CC
		private BigNumber SolomonRewards(BigNumber scaleLevel, string additionalParams)
		{
			if (scaleLevel < 20.0)
			{
				return scaleLevel * 5.0;
			}
			if (scaleLevel < 40.0)
			{
				return (scaleLevel - 20.0) * 4.0 + 100.0;
			}
			if (scaleLevel < 60.0)
			{
				return (scaleLevel - 40.0) * 3.0 + 180.0;
			}
			if (scaleLevel < 80.0)
			{
				return (scaleLevel - 60.0) * 2.0 + 240.0;
			}
			return scaleLevel - 80.0 + 280.0;
		}

		// Token: 0x06000760 RID: 1888 RVA: 0x0001C6D0 File Offset: 0x0001A8D0
		private BigNumber QuadraticSolomon(BigNumber scaleLevel, string additionalParams)
		{
			if (scaleLevel < 20.0)
			{
				return Math.Pow(scaleLevel.ToDouble(), 1.5).Round();
			}
			return Math.Pow(20.0, 1.5).Round() + Math.Pow(scaleLevel.ToDouble() - 20.0, 3.0).Round();
		}

		// Token: 0x06000761 RID: 1889 RVA: 0x0001C754 File Offset: 0x0001A954
		private BigNumber LibAndSiy(BigNumber scaleLevel, string additionalParams)
		{
			BigNumber bn = Controllers.outsidersController.GetIdleBonus() * 0.01 + 1.0;
			if (scaleLevel < 10.0)
			{
				return scaleLevel * 25.0 * bn;
			}
			if (scaleLevel < 20.0)
			{
				return ((scaleLevel - 9.0) * 24.0 + 225.0) * bn;
			}
			if (scaleLevel < 30.0)
			{
				return ((scaleLevel - 19.0) * 23.0 + 465.0) * bn;
			}
			if (scaleLevel < 40.0)
			{
				return ((scaleLevel - 29.0) * 22.0 + 695.0) * bn;
			}
			if (scaleLevel < 50.0)
			{
				return ((scaleLevel - 39.0) * 21.0 + 915.0) * bn;
			}
			if (scaleLevel < 60.0)
			{
				return ((scaleLevel - 49.0) * 20.0 + 1125.0) * bn;
			}
			if (scaleLevel < 70.0)
			{
				return ((scaleLevel - 59.0) * 19.0 + 1325.0) * bn;
			}
			if (scaleLevel < 80.0)
			{
				return ((scaleLevel - 69.0) * 18.0 + 1515.0) * bn;
			}
			if (scaleLevel < 90.0)
			{
				return ((scaleLevel - 79.0) * 17.0 + 1695.0) * bn;
			}
			if (scaleLevel < 100.0)
			{
				return ((scaleLevel - 89.0) * 16.0 + 1865.0) * bn;
			}
			return ((scaleLevel - 99.0) * 15.0 + 2025.0) * bn;
		}

		// Token: 0x06000762 RID: 1890 RVA: 0x0001CA3C File Offset: 0x0001AC3C
		private BigNumber AscendGoldAmount(BigNumber scaleLevel, string additionalParams)
		{
			int[] array = new int[]
			{
				0,
				50,
				250,
				1000,
				4000,
				20000,
				100000,
				400000,
				2500000,
				15000000,
				100000000,
				800000000
			};
			if (scaleLevel > (double)(array.Length - 1))
			{
				return new BigNumber((double)array[array.Length - 1]);
			}
			return new BigNumber((double)array[(int)scaleLevel.ToDouble()]);
		}

		// Token: 0x06000764 RID: 1892 RVA: 0x0001CAC0 File Offset: 0x0001ACC0

			double num = double.Parse(array[0]);
			double num2 = double.Parse(array[1]);
			return new BigNumber(num * (1.0 - Math.Exp(scaleLevel.ToDouble() * num2)));
		}

﻿using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;

namespace Logic.Models
{
	// Token: 0x020000B7 RID: 183
	public class DynamicCollectionContainerModel : Model
	{
		// Token: 0x0600076F RID: 1903 RVA: 0x0001CCBE File Offset: 0x0001AEBE
		public DynamicCollectionContainerModel()
		{
			this._currentUids = new Dictionary<string, uint>();
		}

		// Token: 0x06000770 RID: 1904 RVA: 0x0001CCD4 File Offset: 0x0001AED4
		public uint AppendToCollection<T>(string collection, T child, Dictionary<uint, T> dict)
		{
			if (!this._currentUids.ContainsKey(collection))
			{
				this._currentUids.Add(collection, 1U);
			}
			uint num = this._currentUids[collection];
			if (dict.ContainsKey(num))
			{
				throw new Exception(string.Concat(new string[]
				{
					"Someone already put ",
					num.ToString(),
					" in collection ",
					collection,
					" and now the UID generator is out of sync."
				}));
			}
			Dictionary<string, uint> currentUids = this._currentUids;
			uint num2 = currentUids[collection];
			currentUids[collection] = num2 + 1U;
			dict.Add(num, child);
			return num;
		}

		// Token: 0x040007E2 RID: 2018
		[Model.SavedAttribute]
		private Dictionary<string, uint> _currentUids;
	}
}

		protected BigNumber Polynomial1_5PartialSum(BigNumber x, string additionalParams)
		{
			x += 1.0;
			BigNumber bigNumber = BigNumber.Sqrt(x);
			BigNumber bigNumber2 = x * bigNumber;
			BigNumber bn = x * bigNumber2 * 0.4;
			BigNumber bn2 = bigNumber2 * 0.5;
			BigNumber bn3 = bigNumber * 0.125;
			BigNumber bn4 = 0.00052 / bigNumber2;

			this.heroes = new Dictionary<uint, HeroModel>();
			this.maxSize = 256U;
			uint[] allIDs = StaticData.GetAllIDs<HeroData>();
			uint num = 0U;
			foreach (uint num2 in allIDs)
			{
				num += 1U;
				HeroModel value = new HeroModel
				{
					id = num2,
					uid = num
				};

			}
		}

		private BigNumber SolomonRewards(BigNumber scaleNumber, string additionalParams)
		{
			if (scaleNumber < 20.0)
			{
				return scaleNumber * 5.0;
			}
			if (scaleNumber < 40.0)
			{
				return 100 + (scaleNumber - 20.0) * 4.0;
			}
			if (scaleNumber < 60.0)
			{
				return 180 + (scaleNumber - 40.0) * 3.0;
			}
			if (scaleNumber < 80.0)
			{
				return 240 + (scaleNumber - 60.0) * 2.0;
			}
			return 280 + (scaleNumber - 80.0);
		}

			return 2025 + (scaleNumber - 99.0) * 15.0;

		// Token: 0x060007BE RID: 1982 RVA: 0x0001D9A0 File Offset: 0x0001BBA0
		private BigNumber QuadraticSolomon(BigNumber scaleNumber, string additionalParams)
		{
			if (scaleNumber < 20.0)

			return Math.Pow(20.0, 1.5).Round() + Math.Pow(scaleNumber.ToDouble() - 20.0, 3.0).Round();
		}

		// Token: 0x060007BF RID: 1983 RVA: 0x0001DA24 File Offset: 0x0001BC24

			}
			return ItemBonusTypeModel.ASCENT_GOLD_VALUES[scaleNumber.ToInt()];
		}

		// Token: 0x060007E3 RID: 2019 RVA: 0x0001E8CA File Offset: 0x0001CACA
		public Random()
		{
			this.seed = 0L;
			this.numUses = 0U;
		}

		// Token: 0x060007E4 RID: 2020 RVA: 0x0001E8E4 File Offset: 0x0001CAE4
		public long Rand()
		{
			if (this.seed == 0L)
			{
				throw new InvalidOperationException("Rand() called without a seed");
			}
			this.numUses += 1U;
			this.seed = this.seed * 16807L % 2147483647L;
			return this.seed;
		}

		// Token: 0x060007E5 RID: 2021 RVA: 0x0001E932 File Offset: 0x0001CB32
		public float RandFloat()
		{
			return (float)this.Rand() * 1f / 2.1474836E+09f;
		}

		private int SortWeightedChoices<T>(Random.WeightedChanceStruct<T> a, Random.WeightedChanceStruct<T> b)
		{
			if (a.weight < b.weight)
			{
				return -1;
			}
			if (a.weight > b.weight)
			{
				return 1;
			}
			return 0;
		}

		// Token: 0x060007F0 RID: 2032 RVA: 0x0001EA10 File Offset: 0x0001CC10
		public T WeightedChoice<T>(Dictionary<T, uint> dictionary)
		{
			uint num = 0U;
			List<Random.WeightedChanceStruct<T>> list = new List<Random.WeightedChanceStruct<T>>();
			foreach (T t in dictionary.Keys)
			{
				if (dictionary[t] != 0U)
				{
					num += dictionary[t];
					list.Add(new Random.WeightedChanceStruct<T>
					{
						obj = t,
						weight = dictionary[t]
					});
				}
			}
			if (num == 0U)
			{
				throw new InvalidOperationException("Sum of weightedChoice options does not add up to anything meaningful");
			}
			list.Sort(new Comparison<Random.WeightedChanceStruct<T>>(this.SortWeightedChoices<T>));
			long num2 = this.Rand() % (long)((ulong)(num + 1U));
			num = 0U;
			foreach (Random.WeightedChanceStruct<T> weightedChanceStruct in list)
			{
				num += weightedChanceStruct.weight;
				if (num2 <= (long)((ulong)num))
				{
					return weightedChanceStruct.obj;
				}
			}
			throw new InvalidOperationException("Argument passed to Random.weightedChoice is invalid");
		}

			// Token: 0x04000D25 RID: 3365

			{
				rand.SRand(seed);
			}
		}

				this.autoclickerSkins = new Dictionary<uint, bool>
				{
					{
						1U,
						true
					}
				};
			}
			if (this.heroOrangeFishRewarded == null)
			{
				this.heroOrangeFishRewarded = new Dictionary<uint, uint>();
			}
			if (this.skillCooldowns == null)
			{
				this.skillCooldowns = new Dictionary<uint, long>();
			}
			if (this.usedSkills == null)
			{
				this.usedSkills = new Dictionary<uint, bool>();
			}
			if (this.purchaseRecord == null)
			{
				this.purchaseRecord = new Dictionary<string, uint>();
			}
			if (this.upgrades == null)
			{
				this.upgrades = new Dictionary<uint, bool>();
			}
			if (this.devGifts == null)
			{
				this.devGifts = new Dictionary<uint, uint>();
			}
			if (this.collectedRaidRewardDates == null)
			{
				this.collectedRaidRewardDates = new Dictionary<string, bool>();
			}
			if (this.appliedDLC == null)
			{
				this.appliedDLC = new Dictionary<uint, bool>();
			}
			if (this.privateAdminMessages == null)
			{
				this.privateAdminMessages = new Dictionary<uint, PrivateAdminMessageModel>();
			}
			if (this.settings == null)
			{
				this.settings = new Dictionary<string, string>();
			}
			if (this.offers == null)
			{
				this.offers = new OffersModel();
			}
			if (this.outsiders == null)
			{
				this.outsiders = new OutsidersModel();
			}
			if (this.ancients == null)
			{
				this.ancients = new AncientsModel();
			}
			if (this.items == null)
			{
				this.items = new ItemsModel();
			}
			if (this.heroCollection == null)
			{
				this.heroCollection = new HeroesModel();
			}
			if (this.mercenaries == null)
			{
				this.mercenaries = new MercenariesModel();
			}
			if (this.newImmortalResults == null)
			{
				this.newImmortalResults = new NewImmortalResults();
			}
			if (this.purchaseHistory == null)
			{
				this.purchaseHistory = new PurchaseHistoryModel();
			}
			if (this.persistentVars == null)
			{
				this.persistentVars = new PersistentVarsModel();
			}
			if (this.personalSales == null)
			{
				this.personalSales = new SalesModel();
			}
			if (this.stats == null)
			{
				this.stats = new StatsModel();
			}
			if (this.account == null)
			{
				this.account = new AccountModel();
			}
			MercenariesModel mercenariesModel = this.mercenaries;
			if (mercenariesModel.questRoller == null)
			{
				mercenariesModel.questRoller = new Random();
			}
			this.ValidateSeed(this.mercenaries.questRoller, (this.creationTimestamp + 222222L) % 2147483646L);
			mercenariesModel = this.mercenaries;
			if (mercenariesModel.mercRoller == null)
			{
				mercenariesModel.mercRoller = new Random();
			}
			this.ValidateSeed(this.mercenaries.mercRoller, (this.epicRoller.seed + 111111L) % 2147483646L);
			mercenariesModel = this.mercenaries;
			if (mercenariesModel.mercNameRoller == null)
			{
				mercenariesModel.mercNameRoller = new Random();
			}
			this.ValidateSeed(this.mercenaries.mercNameRoller, (this.epicRoller.seed + 111111L) % 2147483646L);
			ItemsModel itemsModel = this.items;
			if (itemsModel.ascensionItemsRoller == null)
			{
				itemsModel.ascensionItemsRoller = new Random();
			}
			this.ValidateSeed(this.items.ascensionItemsRoller, this.creationTimestamp % 2147483646L);
			itemsModel = this.items;
			if (itemsModel.guildItemsRoller == null)
			{
				itemsModel.guildItemsRoller = new Random();
			}
			this.ValidateSeed(this.items.guildItemsRoller, this.creationTimestamp % 2147483646L);
			itemsModel = this.items;
			if (itemsModel.bonusZoneRoller == null)
			{
				itemsModel.bonusZoneRoller = new Random();
			}
			this.ValidateSeed(this.items.bonusZoneRoller, this.creationTimestamp % 2147483646L);
			this.sortAncientsByName = Platform.IsMobileDisplay();
		}
